Make 10 requests (at the limit)\n        for _ in range(10):\n            response = middleware(request)\n            self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n    @override_settings(RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS=3, RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW=60)\n    def test_request_exceeds_limit(self):\n        \"\"\"Requests exceeding the rate limit should return 429.\"\"\"\n        middleware = RateLimitMiddleware(get_response)\n        request = self.rf.get(\"/\")\n        request.META[\"REMOTE_ADDR\"] = \"192.168.1.2\"\n\n        # Make 3 requests (within limit)\n        for _ in range(3):\n            response = middleware(request)\n            self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n        # 4th request should be rate limited\n        response = middleware(request)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 429)\n\n    @override_settings(RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS=5, RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW=60)\n    def test_cache_isolation_per_ip(self):\n        \"\"\"Different IPs should have isolated rate limit counters.\"\"\"\n        middleware = RateLimitMiddleware(get_response)\n\n        # IP 1 makes 5 requests\n        request1 = self.rf.get(\"/\")\n        request1.META[\"REMOTE_ADDR\"] = \"192.168.1.100\"\n        for _ in range(5):\n            response = middleware(request1)\n            self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n        # IP 1's 6th request should be rate limited\n        response = middleware(request1)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 429)\n\n        # IP 2 should still be able to make requests\n        request2 = self.rf.get(\"/\")\n        request2.META[\"REMOTE_ADDR\"] = \"192.168.1.101\"\n        response = middleware(request2)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n    @override_settings(RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS=100, RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW=3600)\n    def test_default_settings(self):\n        \"\"\"Middleware should use default settings if not overridden.\"\"\"\n        middleware = RateLimitMiddleware(get_response)\n        request = self.rf.get(\"/\")\n        request.META[\"REMOTE_ADDR\"] = \"192.168.1.3\"\n\n        # Should handle 100 requests (default limit)\n        for _ in range(100):\n            response = middleware(request)\n            self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 200)\n\n        # 101st request should be rate limited\n        response = middleware(request)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 429)\n\n    @override_settings(RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS=2, RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW=60)\n    def test_rate_limit_429_response(self):\n        \"\"\"Rate limited response should have proper status code.\"\"\"\n        middleware = RateLimitMiddleware(get_response)\n        request = self.rf.get(\"/\")\n        request.META[\"REMOTE_ADDR\"] = \"192.168.1.4\"\n\n        # Use up the limit\n        for _ in range(2):\n            middleware(request)\n\n        # Next request should be rate limited\n        response = middleware(request)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 429)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(response.content)\n\n    def test_missing_remote_addr(self):\n        \"\"\"Middleware should handle missing REMOTE_ADDR gracefully.\"\"\"\n        middleware = RateLimitMiddleware(get_response)\n        request = self.rf.get(\"/\")\n        # Don't set REMOTE_ADDR\n\n        # Should still work with a default or empty string\n        response = middleware(request)\n        # Should not crash and should return 200\n        self.assertIn(response.status_code, [200, 429])\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1618,"cache_read_input_tokens":31377,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1618},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e4b4dba5-62d1-4c87-a188-6c9594ffc74d","uuid":"bd632557-620f-45b2-a5d7-8bcf0cf7fb69"}

RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: Maximum requests per window (default: 100)\n    - RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: Time window in seconds (default: 3600)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, get_response):\n        super().__init__(get_response)\n        self.rate_limit_requests = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS\", 100)\n        self.rate_limit_window = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW\", 3600)\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client has exceeded the rate limit.\n\n        Returns a 429 response if the limit is exceeded, None otherwise.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Get the client's IP address\n        client_ip = request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"\")\n\n        # Create a cache key for this IP\n        cache_key = f\"ratelimit:{client_ip}\"\n\n        # Get the current request count\n        request_count = cache.get(cache_key, 0)\n\n        # Check if the limit has been exceeded\n        if request_count >= self.rate_limit_requests:\n            return HttpResponseTooManyRequests(\"Rate limit exceeded\")\n\n        # Increment the request count and set the timeout\n        cache.set(cache_key, request_count + 1, self.rate_limit_window)\n\n        # Allow the request to proceed\n        return None\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":550,"cache_read_input_tokens":35753,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":550},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e4b4dba5-62d1-4c87-a188-6c9594ffc74d","uuid":"a5dea505-f414-4fa1-87c2-bed8910c37e7"}

RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: Maximum requests per window (default: 100)\n    - RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: Time window in seconds (default: 3600)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, get_response):\n        super().__init__(get_response)\n        self.rate_limit_requests = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS\", 100)\n        self.rate_limit_window = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW\", 3600)\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client has exceeded the rate limit.\n\n        Returns a 429 response if the limit is exceeded, None otherwise.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Get the client's IP address\n        client_ip = request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"\")\n\n        # Create a cache key for this IP\n        cache_key = f\"ratelimit:{client_ip}\"\n\n        # Get the current request count\n        request_count = cache.get(cache_key, 0)\n\n        # Check if the limit has been exceeded\n        if request_count >= self.rate_limit_requests:\n            return HttpResponseTooManyRequests(\"Rate limit exceeded\")\n\n        # Increment the request count and set the timeout\n        cache.set(cache_key, request_count + 1, self.rate_limit_window)\n\n        # Allow the request to proceed\n        return None\n","numLines":53,"startLine":1,"totalLines":53}}}
